			}

			add_character_modifier = { name = has_two_faiths_modif days = -1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = japan_group
						capital_scope = {
							region = world_japan
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = asia.76 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = korean_group
						capital_scope = {
							region = world_korea
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = asia.86 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = viet
						culture_group = chamic
						culture_group = bahnaric
						capital_scope = {
							region = world_vietnam
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = asia.96 }
			}
			else = {
				character_event = { id = asia.66 }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

					gain_empire_effect = yes
				}

				}

			}
		}

			factor = 1
		}

	form_visegrad = {
		is_high_prio = yes
		only_playable = yes
		ai_check_interval = 36
		potential = {
			form_empire_potential = yes
			OR = {		###Must be one of the following cultures
				culture_group = magyar
				culture_group = west_slavic
			}
			e_carpathia = {
				is_titular = yes
				has_holder = no
			}
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
		}

		allow = {
			form_empire_allow = yes
			#Control Czech, Poland & Slovakia
				k_poland = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				k_hungary = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_slovakia = { is_titular = no } }
					k_slovakia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_bohemia = { is_titular = no } }
					k_bohemia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_czechoslovakia = { is_titular = no } }
					k_czechoslovakia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_wendia = { is_titular = no } }
					k_wendia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_silesia = { is_titular = no } }
					k_silesia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				conditional_tooltip = {
					trigger = { k_gorale = { is_titular = no } }
					k_gorale = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
		}

		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = form_visegrad_tt
				e_carpathia = {
					gain_empire_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = yes
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = visegrad_female
				}
				new_bloodline = {
					set_description = "visegrad_female_desc"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = no
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = visegrad_male
				}
				new_bloodline = {
					set_description = "visegrad_male_desc"
				}
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				k_poland = { de_jure_liege = e_carpathia }
				e_carpathia = {
					k_slovakia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_bohemia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_czechoslovakia 	= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_wendia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_hungary 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_silesia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_gorale 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
				}
				ROOT = {
					narrative_event = { id = ATEOW_realm_event.99999 }
				}
				any_playable_ruler = {
					narrative_event = { id = ATEOW_realm_event.99999 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	restore_hungary = {#####Hungry Hungry Hungary
		is_high_prio = yes
		only_playable = no
		ai_check_interval = 36
		potential = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = restored_hungary
			}
			has_landed_title = k_hungary
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
		}

		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = all_relevant_titles_must_be_owned_or_owned_by_vassals_tt
			}
			form_kingdom_allow = yes
			prestige = 500
			#Controls a bunch of shit
				d_transylvania = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				d_ungvar = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				d_nyitra = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				d_esztergom = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
		}

		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = restore_hungary_tt
			}
			prestige = -500
			set_global_flag = restored_hungary
			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_transylvania = { de_jure_liege = k_hungary }
				d_ungvar = { de_jure_liege = k_hungary }
				d_nyitra = { de_jure_liege = k_hungary }
				d_esztergom = { de_jure_liege = k_hungary }
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	form_cornwall = {
			
		is_high_prio = yes
		only_playable = no
		ai_check_interval = 36
		potential = {
			form_kingdom_potential = yes
			OR = {	
				culture = cornish
				has_landed_title = e_tirnanog
			}
			k_cornwall = {
				is_titular = yes
				has_holder = no
			}
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
		}

		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = all_relevant_titles_must_be_owned_or_owned_by_vassals_tt
			}
			form_kingdom_allow = yes
			#Controls a bunch of shit
				d_somerset = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				d_hampshire = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				d_cornwall = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
		}

		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = form_cornwall_tt
				k_cornwall = {
					gain_title_effect = yes
				}
			}
			

			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_cornwall = { de_jure_liege = k_cornwall }
				d_hampshire = { de_jure_liege = k_cornwall }
				d_somerset = { de_jure_liege = k_cornwall }
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	form_great_russia = {
		is_high_prio = yes
		only_playable = yes
		ai_check_interval = 36
		potential = {
			form_empire_potential = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = east_slavic
				culture_group = far_east_slavic
			}
			e_great_russia = {
				has_holder = no
			}
			NOR = {
				religion = stalinist
				religion = trotskyite
				religion = leninist
			}
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
		}

		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = all_relevant_titles_must_be_owned_or_owned_by_vassals_tt
			}
			form_empire_allow = yes
			#Control Russian Kingdoms
			k_chernigov = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_pietropolis = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_vladimir = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_volgaria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					k_perm = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_arkhangelsk = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					k_alania = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_ossetia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_ingushetia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_circassia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_balkaria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_donkuban = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_caspia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_povolzhye = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_chechnya = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			k_smalensk = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			conditional_tooltip = {
				trigger = { k_belarus = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia } }
				k_belarus = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			}
			e_cccp = {
				OR = {
					has_holder = no
					is_titular = yes
				}
			}
		}

		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = form_great_russia_tt
				e_great_russia = {
					gain_empire_effect = yes
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = yes
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = great_russia_female
				}
				new_bloodline = {
					set_description = "great_russia_female_desc"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = no
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = great_russia_male
				}
				new_bloodline = {
					set_description = "great_russia_male_desc"
				}
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				###Russia unites!
				k_chernigov = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				k_pietropolis = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				k_vladimir = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				k_volgaria = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				k_smalensk = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_belarus = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_belarus = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_perm = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_perm = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_arkhangelsk = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_arkhangelsk = { de_jure_liege = e_great_russia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_alania = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }

				}
				if = {

	form_cccp = {
		is_high_prio = yes
		only_playable = yes
		ai_check_interval = 36
		potential = {
			form_empire_potential = yes
			OR = {
				religion = stalinist
				religion = leninist
				religion = trotskyite
				religion = cosmist
			}

			e_cccp = {
				has_holder = no
			}
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
		}

		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = all_relevant_titles_must_be_owned_or_owned_by_vassals_tt
			}
			form_empire_allow = yes
			#Control Russian Kingdoms
			k_chernigov = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_pietropolis = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_vladimir = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			k_volgaria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					k_perm = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_arkhangelsk = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					k_alania = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_ossetia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_ingushetia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_circassia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_balkaria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_donkuban = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_caspia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_povolzhye = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
					k_chechnya = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			k_smalensk  = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			conditional_tooltip = {
				trigger = { k_belarus = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp } }
				k_belarus = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes }
			}
			e_great_russia = {
				OR = {
					has_holder = no
					is_titular = yes
				}
			}
		}

		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = form_cccp_tt
				e_cccp = {
					gain_empire_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { religion = stalinist }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_female
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_female_desc"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_male
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_male_desc"
					}
				}
				stalinist = {
					make_reformer_head_of_religion = yes
					set_religion_head = e_cccp
				}
				activate_title = { title = d_stalinist  status = no }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { religion = trotskyite }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_female_trotskyite
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_female_trotskyite_desc"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_male_trotskyite
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_male_trotskyite_desc"
					}
				}
				trotskyite = {
					make_reformer_head_of_religion = yes
					set_religion_head = e_cccp
				}
				activate_title = { title = d_trotskyite  status = no }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { religion = leninist }
				add_trait = leninov
				any_child_even_if_dead = {
					add_trait = leninov
				}
				character_event = { id = LENIN.1000 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_female_leninist
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_female_leninist_desc"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_male_leninist
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_male_leninist_desc"
					}
				}
				leninist = {
					make_reformer_head_of_religion = yes
					set_religion_head = e_cccp
				}
				activate_title = { title = d_leninist  status = no }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { religion = cosmist }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_female_cosmist
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_female_cosmist_desc"
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
					}
					create_bloodline = {
						type = cccp_male_cosmist
					}
					new_bloodline = {
						set_description = "cccp_male_cosmist_desc"
					}
				}
				cosmist = {
					make_reformer_head_of_religion = yes
					set_religion_head = e_cccp
				}
				activate_title = { title = d_cosmist  status = no }
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				###CCCP unites!
				k_chernigov = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				k_pietropolis = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				k_vladimir = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				k_volgaria = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				k_smalensk = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_belarus = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_belarus = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_perm = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_perm = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_arkhangelsk = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_arkhangelsk = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_alania = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_alania = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_donkuban = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_donkuban = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_kalmykia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_kalmykia = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_bashkiria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_bashkiria = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_balkaria = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_balkaria = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_circassia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_circassia = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						k_ingushetia = {  province_completely_controls_trigger = yes } 
					}
					k_ingushetia = { de_jure_liege = e_cccp }
				}

		}

				e_austria_romaia = {
					k_bohemia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_slovakia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_slovenia 			= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }
					k_chorwatia 		= { set_de_jure_if_controls_effect = yes }

				# 	narrative_event = { id = ATEOW_realm_event.99998 }
				# }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = yes
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = austria_romaia_female
				}
				new_bloodline = {
					set_description = "austria_romaia_female_desc"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_female = no
					has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
				}

					type = austria_romaia_male
				}

		}

		}

	gifts_to_people = {
		only_playable = yes
		ai_check_interval = 2

		potential = {
			is_playable = yes
			  OR = {
                is_feudal = yes
                is_tribal = yes
                is_nomadic = yes
            }
			prisoner = no
			has_regent = no
			primary_title = { title = e_bhutan }
			NOT = {	has_character_modifier = celebrated_gifts_to_people }
		}
		allow = {
			war = no
			wealth = 4000
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = is_not_busy_trigger_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = { NOT = { has_character_flag = do_not_disturb } }
			}
		}
		effect = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = celebrated_gifts_to_people
				duration = 364
				hidden = yes
			}			
			set_character_flag = recent_minor_decision
			set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 36999 days = 150 } } # Safety catch flag clearing
			hidden_tooltip = { 
				character_event = { id = bhutan.7  }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = capital_prospers_custom_tooltip
					hidden_tooltip = {
						capital_scope = {
							change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 8 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_flag = recent_minor_decision
				NOT = {
					had_character_flag = {
						flag = recent_minor_decision
						days = 730
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
